<div id="review_1344961900" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1344961900" />
    <a title="Emmeline (The Book Herald)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/16530110-emmeline-the-book-herald"><img alt="Emmeline (The Book Herald)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1599888119p2/16530110.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1344961900?book_show_action=true">Jul 25, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Emmeline (The Book Herald)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Emmeline (The Book Herald)" href="/user/show/16530110-emmeline-the-book-herald">Emmeline (The Book Herald)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16530110-emmeline-the-book-herald?shelf=paranormal">paranormal</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16530110-emmeline-the-book-herald?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16530110-emmeline-the-book-herald?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16530110-emmeline-the-book-herald?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16530110-emmeline-the-book-herald?shelf=book-boyfriends">book-boyfriends</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16530110-emmeline-the-book-herald?shelf=epic">epic</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16530110-emmeline-the-book-herald?shelf=best-world-building">best-world-building</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16530110-emmeline-the-book-herald?shelf=favourite-series">favourite-series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16530110-emmeline-the-book-herald?shelf=adventure">adventure</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16530110-emmeline-the-book-herald?shelf=strong-female-character">strong-female-character</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1344961900" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16647364009202152849"><i>I received a copy of this book from 47North Amazon Publishing via NG in return for an honest review!</i><br/><br/><b>THIS BOOK WAS AMAZING!!</b><br/><br/>This was this easiest 5 stars that i've given to a book in a while. <br/>I didn't question it.<br/>I had no need to second guess myself.<br/>It's a 5 star for sure!! <br/><br/>Okay I'm going to be jumping straight into it and write a rendition of the plot!<br/><br/><i>
  <b>"We stand together as a unified force of destiny. In this , Our most monumental moment, we teeter upon the precipice of a new dawn: the rise of</b></i></span>
  <span id="freeText16647364009202152849" style="display:none"><i>I received a copy of this book from 47North Amazon Publishing via NG in return for an honest review!</i><br /><br /><b>THIS BOOK WAS AMAZING!!</b><br /><br />This was this easiest 5 stars that i've given to a book in a while. <br />I didn't question it.<br />I had no need to second guess myself.<br />It's a 5 star for sure!! <br /><br />Okay I'm going to be jumping straight into it and write a rendition of the plot!<br /><br /><i>
  <b>"We stand together as a unified force of destiny. In this , Our most monumental moment, we teeter upon the precipice of a new dawn: the rise of the House of Alameeda."</b>
</i><br /><br /><blockquote>
  <i>In a land beyond time and space,<br />between the vast equilibrium of time,<br />beyond the knowledge of dimensions,<br />Ethar rises. <br />The five houses: Alameeda, Wurthem, Peney, Comantre, and Rafe are doomed. <br /><b>"One House of Ethar will fall...One House will rule."</b><br />The Fate of Rafe and Alameeda are blurred in the ashes of war and obsession. <br />One thing they desire above all.<br />To possess the child born of the two houses,<br />the child who has the gift of precognition. <br />Kricket will have to fight or be used by the whims of men,<br />One thing is for sure, she will not be separated from Trey, <br />She will kill anyone who stands in her way.<br />There may be a sea of stars but this ocean is one Kricket will concur to survive.</i>
</blockquote><br /><br />Sorry I had to make it all dramatic!<br /><br />Oh my goodness this book! <br />Wow, wow, wow. <br /><br />Boy am I glad to have kept going with this story! <br />Bartol I applaud you and your beautiful imagination! <br /><br />This book was everything I love in a story and more, there is a romance that makes my heart sing, there is a love character (Trey) that I wish was real and is now in my book- boyfriends list. There is adventure and action, there is so much intrigue and machinations that it boggles my mind when i attempt to think of what is next! <br /><br />I love this book, I love this book. <br /><br />Kricket has got to be hands down one of my ultimate favourite characters. Hands down. <br />Her sarcasm and unbelievable ingenuity makes her one of the most appealing and amazing character. <br /><br />I'm sorry, I know I sound like I'm having a gush-fest but honestly, these books are the boss. <br /><br />Trey...oh, my Trey, why can't you be real? *wipes drool* <br />Now this is a romance I love!<br /><br /><b>
  <i>"You are the brightest star among the Sea of Stars, Kricket."</i>
</b><br /> <br />Being willing to die for the person you love, to be with them, to fight for them. To never give up on each other. That's the kind of love you can expect.<br /><br /><b>
  <i>"If this doesn't work out for us, Kricket, know that i've loved you from the moment I held you in my arms on Ethar, and every moment in between. I will love you even after my final breath.'</i>
</b><br /><br />If that didn't make you swoon, and sigh, my goodness there may be something wrong with either you... or me. I'm betting on me <br /><br />Side note- This is very much of a New Adult book, however, Bartol did it in a way that I actually Love. When there was a *cough-cough* scene, she didn't go into detail! bravo! I really liked that, because i don't need to know every detail of that, if you know what I mean.<br /><br />Dang it, I'm gushing again!<br /><br />Anyway, the plot twists in this book, the banter, the love story, the world- building is incredible. <br /><br />I recommend this book with a good- conscience because I know you'll love this book. <br /><br />This didn't have the 2nd book syndrome at all. just saying. It got even better than the first book. <br /><br />Some of my favourite Kricket moments:- <br /><br /><b>
  <i>(kyon)- "I find pleasure in your ability to reason. I'm growing tired of inane blonds."<br />(Kricket)- "That sounds like a cultural hazard for you as an Alameeda. Most of you are pretty stupid."</i>
</b><br /><br /><br /><b>
  <i>"Why is he obsessed with you?"<br />(Kricket)"Who? Kyon? ...well that's simple...I ran away from from him and swore to him that i'd never do anything he says. You should try it sometime. It's called 'I hate you, leave me alone..."</i>
</b><br /><br />God this character makes me laugh! <br /><br />That's all for now my lovelies, you guys just need to read this book! <br /><br />That ending was insanely good too, I'm glad i have a ARC of the 3rd book! hallelujah, i may have lost my mind if i didn't! <br /><br />Stay awesome!<br /><br />-The Book Herald<br /><br /><i>Tweet me <a href="https://twitter.com/TheBookHerald" rel="nofollow noopener">@thebookherald</a><br /></i></span>
  <a data-text-id="16647364009202152849" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_1234086268" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1234086268" />
    <a title="S.E. Anderson" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/32677441-s-e-anderson"><img alt="S.E. Anderson" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1577034855p2/32677441.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1234086268?book_show_action=true">Mar 22, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="S.E. Anderson" class="user" itemprop="url" name="S.E. Anderson" href="/user/show/32677441-s-e-anderson">S.E. Anderson</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/32677441-s-e-anderson?shelf=netgalley">netgalley</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1234086268" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4245949024771997863">I was given an advance copy of this book via NetGalley in exchange for an honest review.<br/><br/>I have to admit... I did not like this novel. Though the world created was fascinating, the characters were incredibly one dimensional. Anyone but Trey and Kricket seemed to have a single character trait (if any), and were somewhat forgettable. <br/><br/>It had a bad case of 'Mary Sue'-itis, with the main protagonist being unrealistic and, admittedly, quite annoying. The reader is constantly dragged away from the plot </span>
  <span id="freeText4245949024771997863" style="display:none">I was given an advance copy of this book via NetGalley in exchange for an honest review.<br /><br />I have to admit... I did not like this novel. Though the world created was fascinating, the characters were incredibly one dimensional. Anyone but Trey and Kricket seemed to have a single character trait (if any), and were somewhat forgettable. <br /><br />It had a bad case of 'Mary Sue'-itis, with the main protagonist being unrealistic and, admittedly, quite annoying. The reader is constantly dragged away from the plot as Kricket incessantly reminds us how attractive and sexy Trey is. And we're always reminded how perfect Kricket is, how attractive she is even though she's so very short, how intelligent and amazing she is - oh, right, she just can't swim! Every five pages or so someone reminds us how smart she is, or how she's perfect at everything she tries. I feel like Kricket could have been a strong character, if she only had more depth than just "perfect and oh so meek about her perfection". She could have even been a little badass. There are some moments when it feel it in her, but then... sigh... we get sidetracked.<br /><br />And then there is the fact that she's constantly reminding us how platinum blond her hair is. Or how she's super attractive and that means everyone hates her for it / fawns over her like she's a kitten. Which Trey calls her often. <br /><br />The plot also annoyingly predictable and repetitive. Kricket sees the future. Enemies attack. They hide. They get separated. Find each other. Now she's hurt, but won't admit it. She may be dying at some points, or be surrounded by war and death, but she remembers to point out how amazing Trev is smelling, or how sultry his voice sounds. I finished the book feeling as if not much had actually happened. The ending itself seemed rushed, the most interesting part of the book spilling out over the last twenty pages or so, as if the author had just wanted to get us to that point, and used the rest of the novel as a long and winding means to get there. <br /><br />I found the characters shallow and the plot lacking, and the novel suffered from a case of too much exposition as well. Admittedly, I did like the world created, and the visuals described were astounding. Maybe this novel would do better on the screen, as a movie perhaps, or a show. Then more time could be spent on the plot and the intrigue rather than on Trey's attractive sculpted abs. <br /><br />The thing is, i see nothing but glowing reviews for this novel. I'm sorry to be the unpopular opinion. I'll see myself out. </span>
  <a data-text-id="4245949024771997863" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer2712131626034124185">Soooo, book three? Where is it?!?!<br/><br/>I've been waiting for this book for a long time now and I'm so thrilled to have gotten the opportunity to read it a little bit earlier than its release date. Amy Bartol has an impressive gift for writing great stories with even greater romances...So much chemistry and swooniness....my ebook is littered with highlights everywhere!! Trey reminded me once again why he's one of my favourite book boyfriends! Wowzah!<br/><br/>Lovey-dovey-ness aside, Sea of Stars was a solid seq</span>
  <span id="freeText2712131626034124185" style="display:none">Soooo, book three? Where is it?!?!<br /><br />I've been waiting for this book for a long time now and I'm so thrilled to have gotten the opportunity to read it a little bit earlier than its release date. Amy Bartol has an impressive gift for writing great stories with even greater romances...So much chemistry and swooniness....my ebook is littered with highlights everywhere!! Trey reminded me once again why he's one of my favourite book boyfriends! Wowzah!<br /><br />Lovey-dovey-ness aside, Sea of Stars was a solid sequel with tons of action. The ending was crazy and Kricket proved to be stronger than ever. This world and the characters living inside it make me one happy bookworm :)</span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('+iKHAxw8NZT+DXUNwFhzVvEWGP0ad84xf5Gs09EXcziazZPTCBui8yyjP6NRbLMiwJGv46JwcTBPWGLk76k07A==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('b/QOjP4Te4cLECEkwQu4cnU1QvVPM5j72IPNY1JSrokPGxpc6jTs4Nm+a4pQP3gGRLL16/c0J/roSgNUbOzpXQ==')})
  }

  <span id="freeText15852268291382515115" style="display:none">Author of the Secondborn Series:<br />Secondborn (Book 1)<br />Traitor Born (Book 2)<br />Rebel Born (Book 3) <br /><br />Author of the Premonition Series:<br />Inescapable (Book 1) <br />Intuition (Book 2)<br />Indebted (Book 3)<br />Incendiary (Book 4) <br />Iniquity (Book 5) <br /><br />Author of the Kricket Series:<br />Under Different Stars (Book 1) <br />Sea of Stars (Book 2)<br />Darken the Stars (Book 3)<br /><br />The Divided - A Science Fiction Romance short story, which is included in the Take Me To Your Reader: An Otherworld Anthology. <br /><br />Amy A. Bartol is the USA Today and Wall Street Journal bestselling author of The Secondborn Series, The Premonition Series, The Kricket Series, and a short story entitled “The Divided.” She has won numerous awards for her writing and been nominated for several more. She's a graduate of Hillsdale College, which inspired the setting of her Premonition Series. Amy lives in Michigan with her husband and two sons, but she travels often, sparking her imagination to create more worlds like the ones with hidden angels, doorways to alien landscapes, and fantastical futuristic societies and technologies. To learn more, visit Amy's website at: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.amyabartol.com">https://www.amyabartol.com</a></span>
